 5 lakh rupees

 bhartiya rigerv bank (arabiai) ne mangalvaar ko asthai (floating) byaaj dar vaale awaas rin ke paripakv ta avadhi se pehle bhugtan par lagane vaale shulk ko hataane kii ghoshnaa kii
 The Reserve Bank issued a notification in this regard
 bank ke bayaan main kaha gaya ki is shulk ke kaaran rin dharak saste sansadhano kaa upyog nahin kar sakate hai
 The comments bayaan ke mutabik rigerv bank ne kai bainkon ne haal main swechha se asthai byaaj dar vaale awaas rin kii samay purv adaayagi par shulk hataa diya tha, jiske baad sabhi bainkon ke liye samanta sthapit karne kii jarurat thi
 The statement said, "it has therefore been decided that banks will not be allowed to levy fees on the repayment of temporary interest loans with immediate effect
 " The Reserve Bank issued a notification in this regard
 bank ke bayaan main kaha gaya ki is shulk ke kaaran rin dharak saste sansadhano kaa upyog nahin kar sakate hai
 The comments bayaan ke mutabik rigerv bank ne kai bainkon ne haal main swechha se asthai byaaj dar vaale awaas rin kii samay purv adaayagi par shulk hataa diya tha, jiske baad sabhi bainkon ke liye samanta sthapit karne kii jarurat thi
 The statement said, "it has therefore been decided that banks will not be allowed to levy fees on the repayment of temporary interest loans with immediate effect
